10:29:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-17 10:29:49","title":"Marshall Major IV wireless headphones offer great sound, plus 80+ hours of battery life and wireless charging","link":"https://techcrunch.com/?p=2061830","description":"<p id=\"speakable-summary\">Marshall&#8217;s new <a href=\"https://www.marshallheadphones.com/us/en/major-iv.html\">Major IV headphones ($149.99)</a> combine lightweight comfort with wireless charging, and up to 80 hours of playback for an iconic headset that&#8217;s affordable and flexible. At home or on the go, these are a great option with unique features that you won&#8217;t find anywhere else in the headphone market.</p>\n<h2>Basics</h2>\n<p>This is the fourth iteration of Marshall&#8217;s Major on-ear wireless headphones, and they offer a number of improvements new to the lineup, including a new folding clip design that makes them even more compact when packed for travel &#8212; and that allows them to rest comfortably on a charging pad to enable another new feature: wireless charging using the Qi standard.</p>\n<p>Marshall has also greatly improved battery life, advertising an insane 80 hours of usage time on these, way up from the 30+ promised in the last generation. They still feature square earcups with that iconic Marshall look, but the detail on each is flat instead of pebbled faux leather (that remains on the headband). The multi-directional control knob is also carried over from past Major designs, and there&#8217;s a 3.5mm socket for wired sound, and for sharing your audio connection out to another headset.</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<p>In the box, there&#8217;s a coiled 3.5mm cable for that vintage Marshall amp feel, as well as a USB-C cable for wired charging, which will provide a full 80+ hours of use from three hours &#8212; or 15 hours from just 15 minutes with a new quick-charge feature.</p>\n<h2>Design and performance</h2>\n<p>The design of the Major IV is classic Marshall aesthetic &#8212; which is great news. They look fantastic, with the iconic logo in script on both earcups. As mentioned, the earcup face is now smooth and matte, which looks great, and there&#8217;s a silicone edge on each, which helps keep the right earcup in place when placed on a wireless charger.</p>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2061868\" style=\"width: 949px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2061868\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-full wp-image-2061868\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"939\" height=\"639\" srcset=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg 939w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg?resize=150,102 150w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg?resize=300,204 300w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg?resize=768,523 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg?resize=680,463 680w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/04-usp03-major-iv-desktop@1.41x.jpg?resize=50,34 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 939px) 100vw, 939px\" /><p id=\"caption-attachment-2061868\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> Marshall</p></div></p>\n<p>These are compact, over-ear headsets that rest comfortably, and that comfort is helped by the lightweight materials used in their construction. Despite feeling very light, they feel like they&#8217;re made of quality materials thoughtfully constructed, and should last a long time in terms of durability.</p>\n<p>Marshall&#8217;s multi-directional controller is both an attractive cosmetic detail in gold, and a smart control interface that offers intuitive manipulation of audio playback and volume.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"9uO3NH1qO0\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/10/16/shures-aonic-50-wireless-noise-cancelling-headphones-offer-best-in-class-audio-quality/\">Shure&#8217;s Aonic 50 wireless noise-cancelling headphones offer best-in-class audio quality</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Shure&#8217;s Aonic 50 wireless noise-cancelling headphones offer best-in-class audio quality&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/10/16/shures-aonic-50-wireless-noise-cancelling-headphones-offer-best-in-class-audio-quality/embed/#?secret=9uO3NH1qO0\" data-secret=\"9uO3NH1qO0\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>Sound-wise, the Major IV provides great audio quality for a headset in this price range. The bass is rich, and the highs are clear. There&#8217;s no noise cancelling at work here, so you will get a decent amount of audio bleed-in from your surroundings, but they do a decent job of sound isolation for an over-hear set. And the sound quality is made all the better because of the class-leading battery life Marshall has managed to pack into the Major IV. Indeed, 80+ hours is just astounding, and it means you&#8217;ll likely be able to go at least a week or two without even thinking about a charger while using these actively.</p>\n<h2>Bottom line</h2>\n<p>Marshall has really delivered an amazing value with the new Major IV. Combining style, performance and quality into a headset that also has amazing battery life and unique wireless charging capabilities is a true achievement &#8212; and perks like 3.5mm wired audio sharing just round out the package. These are a great everyday headset that you won&#8217;t want to go anywhere without.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/tag/work-from-home-gear\"><img src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/work-from-home-gear-banner.jpg\" /></a></p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a Leaning on the health-tracking capabilities of the Apple Watch, the startup has been aiming to build a platform that teams motivation, accountability and fitness insights.</p><div class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/kleiner-perkins-caufield-byers\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"kleiner-perkins-caufield-byers\">Kleiner Perkins, <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> the startup tells TechCrunch they&#8217;ve closed a $24 million Series B led by <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/trustbridge-partners\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"trustbridge-partners\">Trustbridge Partners, has seen major growth of its own. CEO <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/person/rishi-mandal\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"person\" data-entity=\"rishi-mandal\">Rishi Mandal <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> says that the company&#8217;s growth rate has tripled in recent months as thousands of gyms closed their doors. He says shelter-in-place has merely accelerated an ongoing shift toward tech-forward fitness services that can help busy users find time during their day to exercise.</p>\n<p>”<span class=\"s1\">The operating thesis of the company is that modern life is inherently crazy not just during pandemic times but in normal times,” Mandal says. “The idea of having a set routine is a complete fallacy.”</span></p>\n<p>At $149 per month, Future isn&#8217;t aiming for mass market appeal the same way other digital fitness programs being produced by Peloton, <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/fitbit\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"fitbit\">Fitbit <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> or Apple are. It seems to be more squarely aimed at users who could be a candidate for getting a personal trainer but might not be ready to make the investment or don&#8217;t need the guided instruction so much as they need general guidelines and some accountability.</p>\n<p>As the startup closes on more funding, the team has big goals to expand its network. Mandal aims to have 1,000 coaches on the Future platform by this time next year. Reaching new scales could give the service a chance to tackle new challenges. Mandal sees opportunities for Future to expand its coaching services beyond fitness as it grows, &#8220;There&#8217;s a real opportunity to help people with all aspects of their
